8/17/22, 1:58 PM - Kalla Brahmana: Hello everyone, PFA a link to the match brackets and schedule.

Please read these instructions carefully:
1) Teams have been randomly matched with one another.
2) Team captains will have to be present at the said discord channel 20 mins prior to their match for the map veto. Eg- Match 1: Team captains head to the match 1 channel 
3) Team captains will have to add the admin valorant ID given in the sheet. Admin will then create the custom lobby and invite both captains. Captains will then add the team members to the lobby.
Eg- GD OBSERVER 1 #YKXG (Letters are all caps with the exact spacing)
4) If any team does not show up in the lobby for 10 mins after the said match time, the match will be forfeited and the opponent team will be declared winners. 
5) Any suspicious gameplay will have to be reported to the admin and the rematch will be scheduled accordingly.
6) If there are any technical issues from the players' end, the issue must be resolved within 15 minutes. If the issue isn't resolved and there are only 4 players present, the match will carry on. 
7) No tactical timeouts granted to any teams.

9/7/22, 12:41 PM - Kalla Brahmana: Hello everyone, PFA a link to the match brackets and schedule.

Please read these instructions carefully:
1) Teams have been randomly matched with one another.
2) Team captains will have to be present at the said discord channel 20 mins prior to their match for the map veto. Eg- Match 1: Team captains head to the match 1 channel 
3) Team captains will have to add the admin valorant ID given in the sheet. Admin will then create the custom lobby and invite both captains. Captains will then add the team members to the lobby.
Eg- GD OBSERVER 1 #YKXG (Letters are all caps with the exact spacing)
4) If any team does not show up in the lobby for 10 mins after the said match time, the match will be forfeited and the opponent team will be declared winners. 
5) Any suspicious gameplay will have to be reported to the admin and the rematch will be scheduled accordingly.
6) If there are any technical issues from the players' end, the issue must be resolved within 15 minutes. If the issue isn't resolved and there are only 4 players present, the match will carry on. 
7) No tactical timeouts granted to any teams.
